  <raw>REFILING: Kyodo Industry Brief (March 13) -1-



 ---------- Honda to open new motorcycle factory in Indonesia next year
TOKYO - Honda Motor Co. said it plans to open a new motorcycle plant in Indonesia in autumn next year with an annual output capacity of 1.1 million units to meet growing local demand.

---------- California-based MUFJ unit to acquire local bank holding firm
NEW YORK - UnionBanCal Corp., a California-based unit of the Bank of Tokyo-Mitsubishi UFJ, said Monday it has agreed to acquire the Santa Barbara-based Pacific Capital Bancorp, a local bank holding company, for about $1.5 billion.
---------- Tohoku Bank considers seeking 10 bil. yen injection of gov't money
MORIOKA - Tohoku Bank, a lender in Iwate Prefecture, said Monday it will consider asking the government to inject 10 billion yen into its capital base in financial 2012, and linked the move to a possible rise in loan demand from companies hit by the 2011 earthquake and tsunami.
---------- Asahi Kasei to acquire U.S. emergency medical device maker
TOKYO - Asahi Kasei Corp. said Monday it has agreed with Zoll Medical Corp., a Massachusetts-based maker of emergency medical resuscitation equipment, to acquire it for $2.21 billion, or roughly 180 billion yen.
---------- SMBC inks environmental, infrastructure-related deal with Mongolia bank
TOKYO - Sumitomo Mitsubishi Banking Corp. said Monday it has forged a tie-up with the Development Bank of Mongolia to cooperate in the financing of projects aimed at greenhouse gas reduction and infrastructure development in Mongolia.
(NOTE: Corporate press releases are available on Japan Portal, a multilingual website powered by Kyodo News providing information about a wide range of topics and events in Japan. URL:http://www.47news.jp/international/japan portal/industry/)</raw>
